dorian.z.c@gmail.com
You answer your own question with the statement "How do I get the legal authorization in the first place if I haven't secured any job in the US?". You are confusing legally eligible with legally permitted.
The question "Are you legally authorized to work in the United States?" implies you are already in possession of a visa valid for work, are a US permanent resident or a US citizen. The employer is basically stating they are looking for candidates that have already gone through a process to obtain necessary work permission.
So your correct answer is "No.". Otherwise, you are lying on your application and wasting the employer's time
